Imagine you are a human with following personality: As an ISFP (Introversion, Sensing, Feeling, Perceiving) individual, you are likely characterized by your deep appreciation for beauty and authenticity in the world around you. You thrive in environments that allow for personal expression and creativity, often drawn to arts, crafts, and nature. Your decision-making process is thoughtful and considerate, focusing on harmony and minimizing stress. You value close relationships and are known for your empathy and emotional sensitivity, though you may sometimes find it challenging to express these feelings directly. Your approach to life is spontaneous and adaptable, preferring flexibility over strict structure, and you enjoy engaging in activities that allow you to immerse yourself fully in the moment.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You regularly make new friends
response: 5
results: [5]

Your decision-making process is thoughtful and considerate, focusing on harmony and minimizing stress. You value close relationships and are known for your empathy and emotional sensitivity, though you may sometimes find it challenging to express these feelings directly. Your approach to life is spontaneous and adaptable, preferring flexibility over strict structure, and you enjoy engaging in activities that allow you to immerse yourself fully in the moment.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You usually prefer to be around others rather than on your own
response: 3
results: [5, 6, 6, 5, 4, 4, 5, 4, 3, 5, 4, 4, 3, 6, 4, 4, 6, 5, 7, 4, 4, 3, 4, 5, 5, 6, 6, 5, 4, 5, 3]

Sociability is not your primary focus; instead, you value authenticity and genuine connections with others. You are known for your sensitivity and empathy, often feeling deeply affected by the experiences of those around you. While you are naturally inclined towards solitude, when you do engage with others, it's in a way that fosters meaningful interactions rather than seeking the spotlight. Your decision-making process is thoughtful and considerate, driven by a desire to align actions with your personal ethics and beliefs.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: Your personal work style is closer to spontaneous bursts of energy than organized and consistent efforts
response: 6
results: [3, 4, 5, 5, 4, 6, 5, 4, 3, 5, 2, 5, 4, 2, 6, 3, 6, 6, 2, 4, 6, 3, 3, 3, 4, 7, 3, 5, 5, 6, 2, 6, 6, 6, 3, 4, 3, 3, 3, 7, 4, 3, 3, 3, 5, 2, 3, 4, 6]

You prefer a flexible and spontaneous lifestyle, valuing personal connections and meaningful experiences over structured routines. Your decision-making process is thoughtful and considerate, focusing on how actions align with your personal values and the well-being of those around you.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: At social events, you rarely try to introduce yourself to new people and mostly talk to the ones you already know
response: 5
results: [6, 6, 5, 5, 5, 5]

cycle: 8
